2025 Topps Series 2 Baseball Checklist, Team Set Lists and Details

2025 Baseball Cards, Checklists, Checklists-New
By Andrew Harner - June 25, 2025
June 25, 2025
11
When you click on links to various merchants on this site, like eBay, and make a purchase, this can result in this site earning a commission.
Share:

Jump to the 2025 Topps Series 2 Baseball checklist and team set lists

2025 Topps Series 2 Baseball brings collectors Kings, World Champions, Rickwood Field, and much more.

Keeping with tradition, Topps Series 2 delivers a comprehensive base set with exciting rookies, a rainbow of parallels, plenty of inserts, and plenty of tough pulls to satisfy collectors of all varieties.

2025 Topps Series 2 Baseball Checklist Details

The 2025 Topps Series 2 Baseball base checklist includes 350 cards, which take up slots #s 351-700 on the overall 2025 Topps flagship checklist. Like Series 1, the second series is primarily a mixture of veterans and rookies. There are also two subsets: Future Stars and team cards.

The parallel checklist runs deep, with every card getting dozens of colorful looks. Many parallels utilize special foils, and some exclusives dress up cards with summer themes.

As was done in Series 1, a “First Card” notation will be stamped onto the first example of each Series 2 card that came off the production line.

Every card in the Series 2 set also has a Golden Mirror variation. It’s the third year of these SSPs, but collectors should note the front design of the card does not look different – it is the golden back and alternative photo that make these special.

Inserts, Autographs, Memorabilia and More

It wouldn’t be a Topps flagship set without insert cards.

New inserts include Summer Superstars, OPS Bests, Duos, and All Kings, which honors some of the top hitters from today and year’s past. Pitchers get their due with die-cut K-Zone cards. A short-printed variation displays a reverse K, which is baseball scoring shorthand for when a batter strikes out looking. 

Collectors will also be chasing short-printed Heavy Lumber, Homefield Advantage, and Legendary Homefield Advantage inserts.

The 35th anniversary tribute to 1990 Topps continues with inserts, autographs, and relic cards printed on that year’s flagship design. The base inserts, autographs, and memorabilia cards each have a variety of parallels for collectors to chase. One creative twist is a /35 No Name parallel to the base inserts, a tribute to the famous 1990 Topps NNOF Frank Thomas rookie card. A small number of those cards were printed without Thomas’ name due to a production error.

The Flagship Real One autographs and relic cards return to Series 2, and City Connect Swatches Collection relic and autographed relic cards are also featured.

After winning the 2024 World Series, the Los Angeles Dodgers are featured in a series of single- and dual-signed 2024 World Champion autograph cards, and Topps pays tribute to the MLB game at Alabama’s Rickwood Field with special sets featuring the St. Louis Cardinals.

2025 Topps Series 2 Baseball Silver Packs

2025 Topps Series 2 Baseball again gives collectors silver packs in hobby and jumbo boxes. Standard hobby boxes include one silver pack as a box topper, while jumbo boxes have two packs.

Inside the packs will be mojo-patterned Chrome cards printed on the 1990 Topps design.

2025 Topps Series 2 Baseball cards at a glance:

Cards per pack: Hobby – 12, Jumbo – 40, Mega – 14
Packs per box: Hobby – 20, Jumbo – 10, Mega – 16
Boxes per case: Hobby – 12, Jumbo – 6, Mega – 16
Set size: 350 cards
Release date: June 11, 2025

Shop for 2025 Topps Series 2 Baseball boxes on eBay:

  • Hobby Boxes
  • Jumbo Boxes
  • Mega Boxes
  • Fanatics Fest Boxes

What to expect in a hobby box:

  • Autographs or Memorabilia Cards – 1

What to expect in a jumbo box:

  • Autographs – 1
  • Memorabilia Cards and Other Relics – 2 Total

2025 Topps Series 2 Baseball Checklist

You can also download a customizable spreadsheet copy of the checklist:

  • 2025 Topps Series 2 Baseball Checklist – XLSX File

Please note that print runs for cards without serial numbers have not been announced.

Andrew Harner

Andrew was surrounded by trading cards during adolescence. A lifelong, second-generation collector, he maintains a sizable Tim Salmon collection and has previously published written work with Sports Illustrated, Fanatics, and the Society for American Baseball Research.

  4. Burrion Kemp 25 August, 2025 at 02:46

    The chrome checklist has it in excel format, actually the whole reason I come to becket is for the downloadable Excell checklist, which I think is always here. Doesnt Chrome oome out after Series 2? Will there be an excel, been two months.

  5. Bentley Carpenter 26 September, 2025 at 13:42

    Are the 1/1 first card stamped on the front and the back the 1/1 stamped on the back are they worth anything and how hard are these cards to pull and what boxes do they come out of or do they come in every kind of packs I pulled a mookie Betts out of a retail box so what is the deal with these cards I don’t ever remember these cards over the years I could be wrong

    • Andrew Harner 26 September, 2025 at 15:31

      Hi Bentley,

      That’s an impressive pull! The foil-stamped First Card represents the first card that came off the production line for insertion into packs. These are stamped 1/1 on the back and have very steep pack odds, no matter the configuration. There are multiple retail box types, but the odds of finding a First Card 1/1 for many of the retail offerings are more than 1:60,000 packs.
